<div id="review_421982755" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/421982755" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8179357-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346526379p2/8179357.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/421982755?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/8179357-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8179357-lisa?shelf=loved">loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8179357-lisa?shelf=indie">indie</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer421982755" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13706546890693645534">4.5 Ulcer Inducing Stars! <br/><br/>Rock the Heart was a wild ride through a variety of emotional peaks and valleys. One moment I was happy and then the next I was so freaking mad I snapped at my husband who asked what time I would be starting dinner. Does he not know that when I am reading a good book I could care less about food? Then because I just had to know what happened after a fork went through my heart, I told him I had to “use” the restroom and snuck my iPhone into my hoodie, locked the door and</span>
  <span id="freeText13706546890693645534" style="display:none">4.5 Ulcer Inducing Stars! <br /><br />Rock the Heart was a wild ride through a variety of emotional peaks and valleys. One moment I was happy and then the next I was so freaking mad I snapped at my husband who asked what time I would be starting dinner. Does he not know that when I am reading a good book I could care less about food? Then because I just had to know what happened after a fork went through my heart, I told him I had to “use” the restroom and snuck my iPhone into my hoodie, locked the door and read until my heart was beating at a normal pace again. I love books that do this to me even if my husband does not! Don’t judge…sometimes a girl has to do what a girl has to do to get some reading time! This book had a sweet and salty rock star, a female character I adored and great supporting characters. I loved, loved, loved it!<br /> <br />Lane is right out of college and working on accomplishing her dreams with a career in marketing. She isn’t a risk taker and tends to doubt herself but I loved her because she was NORMAL. She was a down to earth, great girl with the insecurities that most of us face at that age. Though she had doubts and insecurities, she still had amazing strength. She wasn’t a rock groupie or a doormat, just a woman in love with her high school sweetheart. The boy who was her first kiss, her first everything on the dock.<br /> <br /><i>“You are going to be mine again, one day.” – Noel</i><br /> <br />Noel is a rocker and he loves his alcohol and can have any woman he wants. Now, I LOVE french fries with a chocolate shake and Noel was my sweet and salty;) He had the rocker edge and could be an ass but he could also be very cute and romantic. There was a point where his salt outweighed his sweet and I wondered what the heck happened to my Noel. Yes, I can almost guarantee that you will have a love/hate relationship with Noel!<br /> <br /><i>“Because you and I both know this is going to happen. It’s only a matter of time before you give into me.” -Noel</i><br /> <br />I am a firm believer that first loves always hold a special place in your heart. This is true for Noel and Lane but their connection goes deeper than just first love, they are soul mates and compliment each other. They SIZZLE! Now, things did not end well for them back in high school but sometimes in life all we need is a second chance (I think I totally just added a line to a rock song to my review!). Lane has to let go of her doubts and risk her job to make this happen and Noel has to deal with life on the road and things from his past that he is not proud of. As I was reading this, I wanted and needed them to be together. They belong together.<br /> <br />I loved Riff, Trip and Tyke. I am not sure where Michelle got these names but they do fit in with the rock star persona. Trip and Tyke like the ladies but Riff REALLY likes the ladies. He has a little sweet spot for Lane though and even goes as far as to share his Oreos with her! NO ONE gets Riff’s Oreos! Aubrey was a great, supportive friend who was quite different from Lane. She wasn’t as scared to take chances and have a little fun. I can’t wait to read more about these characters!<br /> <br />Now, there is a moment in this one where I felt like someone took my heart out of my chest stomped on it and ran away with it. I expect a little drama in most romance books but WOW and WOW, I did not quite imagine it would be THAT. Yes, for a while there, I didn’t know if Michelle Valentine and I were going to be on speaking terms when I was done with this…How could she do that to me?? I appreciated the emotional roller coaster that was Rock the Heart! It was an exceptional debut and I cannot wait to read the second book in the series, Rock My Bed, which will feature Riff and Aubrey!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13706546890693645534" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14712729113181491068">This is the story of Lane and Noel. They were each other first and only love and best friends since childhood, until when they’re eighteen, Lana break up with Noel because she’s tired of being put in second place, behind his dreams, that she don’t think he can achieve. <br/>Four years later his dreams came true and he’s the lead singer and front man of the one of the best rock bands in the world, the Black Falcon. She is an intern in a big marketing company that wants to score a deal with the band. S</span>
  <span id="freeText14712729113181491068" style="display:none">This is the story of Lane and Noel. They were each other first and only love and best friends since childhood, until when they’re eighteen, Lana break up with Noel because she’s tired of being put in second place, behind his dreams, that she don’t think he can achieve. <br>Four years later his dreams came true and he’s the lead singer and front man of the one of the best rock bands in the world, the Black Falcon. She is an intern in a big marketing company that wants to score a deal with the band. So they send her to do the job, with the promise that she will be fired if something goes wrong. But in order for her to get the contract, he demands that she goes in tour with him and his band for two weeks. <br>So they have to meet again after all this time and soon realize that the feelings that they had once are still there and never disappeared and suddenly all they want is go back in time to a point where they were happy. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420931i/835655.jpg" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They try again from the beginning, with no lies and nothing between them. The problem is that Noel is hiding something that could put everything in danger and afraid to lose her again he tries to hide some things in his life from Lane. She knows she will leave him if she finds out and he is decided to not lose her this time. He wants the forever. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380420931i/835656.jpg" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay, this book was good. Not absolutely amazing, but a very good reading anyway. <br>I can't fully connect with the main characters, especially Lane, first half of the book she is just annoying. Noel was good, although not madly sexy for a rock star. <br>The secondary characters, however, were really good. I liked Riff and Aubrey a LOT. <br>There were several moments where it reminded me a lot of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15724654.The_Mighty_Storm__The_Storm___1_" title="The Mighty Storm (The Storm, #1) by Samantha Towle" rel="nofollow noopener">The Mighty Storm</a>, but TMS was way better. <br>But anyway, it was a good story with rock stars and I'll never grow tired of rock stars stories! ;)<br>I will most certainly read the next ones! </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/6457111-c-c">cεℓтïcεяαƨ мυƨε</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-s-famous">lead-character-s-famous</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=november-2012">november-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=hot-and-heavy">hot-and-heavy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-player">lead-character-player</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=i-want-it-now">i-want-it-now</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=first-love-crush">first-love-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy">lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-rockstar">lead-character-rockstar</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer424146234" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8506889336087076144">Four Stars<br/><br/><b>
  <i>“I’ll do anything you want to make this happen between us, including give you time because I can’t lose you again. It hurts too fucking much.” ~ Noel </i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Son of a bitch!</i> Curse you, Rockgods! You know you’re one of my weaknesses; my kryptonite. I couldn’t help but pick this book up. I seriously have issues. I can’t say no to these hot and sexy tattooed gods. The only thing that would totally make me combust is if he was a British rockstar. Alas, he is not, but that’s okay. Noel Falcon i</span>
  <span id="freeText8506889336087076144" style="display:none">Four Stars<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I’ll do anything you want to make this happen between us, including give you time because I can’t lose you again. It hurts too fucking much.” ~ Noel </i>
</b><br /><br /><i>Son of a bitch!</i> Curse you, Rockgods! You know you’re one of my weaknesses; my kryptonite. I couldn’t help but pick this book up. I seriously have issues. I can’t say no to these hot and sexy tattooed gods. The only thing that would totally make me combust is if he was a British rockstar. Alas, he is not, but that’s okay. Noel Falcon is still one hot male specimen. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>“This next song goes out to the girl who shredded my heart without hesitation back in high school. It’s called Ball Busting Bitch, and Lanie, this one’s for you.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Oh, yea Noel has some resentment towards his former high school love, Lanie. According to Lanie, <i>I knew I broke his heart when I said I could never be with a dreamer because dreams don’t pay the bills.</i> Fast forward four years and now he’s famous. She, however, is still trying to make it in the marketing business. She works as an intern at one of New York’s top marketing companies. Because no one else at the firm volunteers, she reluctantly agrees to wine and dine Noel to obtain information in marketing his charity. This is the kind of break she needed to get hired permanently, but how will she react to seeing Noel? Better yet, how will he react seeing her again?<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“All I want to do is be with you. Now that I have you back I can’t see my life without you. When I think about my future, I think about you.”</i>
</b><br /><br />The love of his life is back. Now that he’s famous, Noel can have anyone he wants. But when Lanie shows up, all he wants her; a second chance. He will do whatever it takes to win her back, including convincing the CEO of her Marketing company to allow her to tour with him and his band while she “researches.” She is not thrilled at this idea and really does not want to subject herself to this. This. Is. Not. Happening. Unfortunately, her career is on the line and she has no choice. Two weeks with Noel. A lot can happen in two weeks.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I tried to get over you. I really did, but you were always there. Every woman I kissed was you.” </i>
</b><br /><br />Second chance love….God, I LOVE stories like this, I’m a sucker for it actually. This story was pretty predictable, but it was still worth the read. Sometimes you need something like this to take you away and live the dream of catching the eye of a super sexy rock star. **sigh** I will always love these type of stories and will always return to them like a moth to a flame. I cannot wait to read book two in the series: Riff and Aubrey’s story. He’s such a man whore and I totally loved Aubrey. I’m also hoping she’ll write one for each twin in the band, too. Tyke and Trip…yumm!! Oh wait! New image is forming in my head: Tyke, Trip and me…**Faints**<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8506889336087076144" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer434131332" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5738457984832018976">I received this book as an ARC from the author. Thank you so much Michelle! You rock!<br/><br/>I don't even know where to begin! I LOVE this book so much that love isn't even an adequate enough word to describe it! It is that good!! <br/>The relationship and attraction between Noel and Lanie is so intense, that you feel yourself being completely consumed by them and their story! If not for my kids, I would have not put this book down until I was done! Even then I only put it down once! <br/>Michelle has you falling</span>
  <span id="freeText5738457984832018976" style="display:none">I received this book as an ARC from the author. Thank you so much Michelle! You rock!<br /><br />I don't even know where to begin! I LOVE this book so much that love isn't even an adequate enough word to describe it! It is that good!! <br />The relationship and attraction between Noel and Lanie is so intense, that you feel yourself being completely consumed by them and their story! If not for my kids, I would have not put this book down until I was done! Even then I only put it down once! <br />Michelle has you falling in love with not just Noel and Lanie, but all of the people you come to meet! Ok so maybe there are a few that you'd like to rip into but strangely you can't because you can understand why things went the way they did. I laughed, cried, had my heart broken, and put back together! Michelle Valentine has written the next big thing! Who can resist these sexy rockers? I sure cant!! I can't wait for Rock My Bed!! Is that not the hottest title ever?!? <br /> This is a MUST READ!! One of my all-time favorite books!! <br />Michelle I wish I could give this book more than 5 stars!! The world needs to know about Noel, Riff, Trip, Tyke, and Striker!! So on the 20th, get it, read it, love it, and tell the world people!!</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oFvZDIYYBOW0t+r92v/q7gya5IK6EDzABMNMQjSGoxpBcqMA41bh5rnMAFzzKhwVwmWXXH1MYECQI7/wASXOAg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/jMkKO54y0MFKPQFCgN6LqTGQ+RTb5d1g3K/Lt+McwwfGl4kizYuQAhTHqQj1ozVajkwOpQzy/UXkkyc6i8eFA==')})
  }
